msg:Stayed at the Temple House in a Studio 90 room. The room exceeded my expectations: it had a refrigerator, including one empty one, a dishwasher, stove, oven, microwave, and washing machine. It even had a kitchen island. Furnishings and bedding were comfortable and there was ample storage space. 

The controls in the room for the lights and drapes were well designed, allowing me to quickly be able to turn the lights on and off without having to fiddle with too many light switches. 

The hotel gym was surprisingly well outfitted for a hotel gym, even including a Smith machine. 

Hotel staff were always around and happy to direct me where I needed to go. I‚Äôve never experienced an attendant draping a towel over me when leaving the pool, but experienced it here. 

The spa is beautiful and the service was excellent. The prices for spa treatments compared favorable to spas in other similar hotels in other cities.

The breakfast buffet was not large but the selection was decent and the quality of the buffet was good. I only wished the room service selection was larger, though room service was generally speedy and tasted very good. 

The hotel location was excellent.

There are also many restaurants, but I don‚Äôt recommend Cuiyuan. The food is not delicious, and the service is average. There is a service fee for normal dishes.
Hotel service
The front desk lady is very enthusiastic. Seeing that it was our first time, she upgraded our room for free. The room facilities and room service are very warm, which is what a high-end hotel should have.
The hotel has its own barber, and guests staying in the hotel can get a 20% discount on haircuts. The master‚Äôs technique is also very good.
There is a Michelin one-star restaurant outside the door, which is opened by the hotel itself, but there is no discount for guests staying in the hotel. The dishes are all vegetarian and the taste is OK. It is just to add a 10% service fee and tax. Friends who mind can buy online in a group, and no service fee is charged. Overall, the service is very good and the service fee is reasonable.
In general, the experience is very good and I will come again next time.

I originally ordered an executive twin bed, but when I checked in, the original room was not cleaned, and the apar**ent suite was upgraded for free.
The original 2K+ one night room was upgraded to 8k+ one night room for free.
Room:
To tell the truth, this room type is really suitable for long-term living, 150 square meters, two bedrooms, each with a separate bathroom. The room is also equipped with a washing machine, a dishwasher, and kitchen utensils are all complete. It is suitable for a family to travel, or for a short-term stay with friends.
Bedding:
The bedding is the most comfortable one I have stayed in so many hotels! ! ! Believe me, lying on the bed, you don't want to get out of bed!
Location:
The Temple House is in Taikoo Li, Chengdu. It is in the business district. Turn right before going out and you can buy it. The first choice for shopping! You can go back to sleep for a while when you are tired, and continue shopping when you wake up. Of course, there are so many delicious food nearby, you can go to the restaurant to get a number, and then go back to the room to wait.
